I can usually get 4, maybe 5 months out of a Sonicare-branded head, but by the end of that time, I'm really noticing that my teeth are not feeling as clean after brushing. I swear the bristles on this one feel the same as the day I started using it!<br /><br />While I'm sure some will consider this to be a plus, I am very concerned because tooth enamel is rather difficult to rebuild once it is lost (some say impossible), and scrubbing it with too hard of a brush can rub it away rather quickly. Given the speed and mechanics of how Sonicare brushes work, I imagine this effect would only be amplified. So I broke down and bought another set of Sonicare branded heads for my HealthyWhite, and will go back to paying through the nose, so that I can rest assured that I have bristles which were meant to be used with a tool of this power.<br /><br />_________UPDATE________<br />After submitting this review, I received a package in the mail from Sonimart.
